5 star service from the Assistant Manager himself!

I had my eyes glued to this Special Edition Tag Heuer Carrera Calibre and wanted it badly as a birthday present to myself. I usually buy my stuff online, but for security reasons, I
hesitated at that time because it was a major purchase.

Unfortunately, even major Department stores and most Authorized Dealers don't carry it which made me want it even more!

After spending countless hours on the internet and days of calling nearby jewelry stores within the Bay area and the Valley, I gave up! None of them will carry the item.

But because I knew I deserve to have one, I resumed and constantly browsed the Tag website in search for an authorized dealer store who can help me, and found Roger's Jewelry Co in Modesto California. It was Todd Evans who answered my phone call who actually wanted the same watch for himself and was very knowledgeable about the product. I went to their store the following morning and he walked me through the buying process, since it's a special edition item, he had to order directly from the manufacturer in Switzerland! I waited at least 4-5 weeks since my watch was still "in production" and tell me about it - It was the longest 5 weeks of my life to say the least! You know that feeling when you know you have a gift under the tree but won't be able to open it until Christmas morning? Todd kept me posted regularly until I received the good news - my watch was ready for pick up! I got it just in time for my birthday! Woohooüòé

Thanks to Todd for a top-notch customer service! Extremely personal and pleasant yet very professional in dealing with his customers! On top of that, he even gave me a great deal for my birthday as well without me even asking!

I would definitely go back and buy again from him! Highly recommended!</Text>

Today, I called Rogers Jewelry needing information on a diamond pendant that I had lost. Sandy was so helpful. She looked up the information on our account and found the item in archives. She did explain that she may not be able to get more information but she would try. Not even a half hour later she had all the information and emailed it to me so I could give it to my insurance company. Thank you so much Sandy.

I feel I need to give a little family history of our relationship with Rogers. My parents bought their wedding sets at Rogers in 1945 and my mom got a new wedding band much later on. My parents bought my 8th grade graduation present, my birthstone ring, from Rogers in 1962 and my high school graduation present, a beautiful watch that I still wear, in 1969. My husband bought my wedding rings at Rogers in 1970. All of these transactions were at the Modesto Rogers Jewelry Store. Of course the locations have changed over the years, their quality and custmer service have always been the best.

We no longer live in California, but always come back to Rogers for our jewelry needs.

Thank you, Rogers Jewelers for always being the best.

< review>
About 2 years ago, I needed a large storage unit for my belongings. Heritage Storage  was the only storage place at that time with the larger units.  At first I thought they were a bit expensive, I had not had this large of a unit before. I left and looked around some more. I did a comparison to Modesto's storages with same large unit.  To my suprise, Heritage was less expensive than Modesto Storages.! And it was close to my home.
I am so happy that I came here for  many reasons.  I like the fact it is gated with a security code. (and if the owners feel there is a safety or security issue, they will change the structure of the code. Which I think is absolutely responsible and smart!)  Heritage is also a very clean business, they are  open 24/7,  and have a great staff. They are not intimidating, they are caring and actually have helped with understanding a financial situation I had.  Vicki who is a wonderful, caring person, helped me by calling me on occasions, and emailing me,  gently reminding me of   due dates and the latest I could pay without compiling late fees or lien fees.I totally appreciated the fact that she  cares!
I would definitely recommend this storage unit for any size storage you need.  The accommodations, and extras and the staff are something you just don't experience with other storage businesses.

Thank you for your great service< /review>

Updates: The "first month free" banner is still up and I have left the facility. My price increased once.

Overall a pretty pleasant experience. I was assisted by Mark who showed me the unit. Up front he disclosed there would be mandatory insurance added on top of the unit fee, and the website disclosed the one time admin fee, so there were no hidden fees by the time I signed the contract/lease. He even warned me ahead of time that the rent would most likely increase in approximately 5 months.

I do have a couple of concerns that lie with the company and its owner. When you drive up, there is a large banner stating "first month free", and upon mentioning it to the employees I am told that this promo is no longer active and they are not allowed to take the banner down. Blatant fishing and false advertisement. Next, I don't know how the units are measured, but I'm renting a 5x5 and when I think that, I think 5 wide x 5 deep. I'm 5'3" and if I were to lie down in the unit I would stick out about halfway. It's more like 2.5 x 2.5.

The prices are a bit high because they take full advantage of the high demand for storage. Based on that I will probably leave the facility before the price goes up.<//text>
